Conclusion: 建议在交叉性视角的软件工程中，公平性评估应包含针对特定模型的缓解策略验证，并在高影响LLM部署中采用工作流级控制（如涉及批评模型的代理架构）；当前结果具有探索性质，可通过扩大数据集规模和应用于其他语言或方言进行扩展。

Abstract: Many works in the literature show that LLM outputs exhibit discriminatory behaviour, triggering stereotype-based inferences based on the dialect in which the inputs are written. This bias has been shown to be particularly pronounced when the same inputs are provided to LLMs in Standard American English (SAE) and African-American English (AAE). In this paper, we replicate existing analyses of dialect-sensitive stereotype generation in LLM outputs and investigate the effects of mitigation strategies, including prompt engineering (role-based and Chain-Of-Thought prompting) and multi-agent architectures composed of generate-critique-revise models. We define eight prompt templates to analyse different ways in which dialect bias can manifest, such as suggested names, jobs, and adjectives for SAE or AAE speakers. We use an LLM-as-judge approach to evaluate the bias in the results. Our results show that stereotype-bearing differences emerge between SAE- and AAE-related outputs across all template categories, with the strongest effects observed in adjective and job attribution. Baseline disparities vary substantially by model, with the largest SAE-AAE differential observed in Claude Haiku and the smallest in Phi-4 Mini. Chain-Of-Thought prompting proved to be an effective mitigation strategy for Claude Haiku, whereas the use of a multi-agent architecture ensured consistent mitigation across all the models. These findings suggest that for intersectionality-informed software engineering, fairness evaluation should include model-specific validation of mitigation strategies, and workflow-level controls (e.g., agentic architectures involving critique models) in high-impact LLM deployments. The current results are exploratory in nature and limited in scope, but can lead to extensions and replications by increasing the dataset size and applying the procedure to different languages or dialects.

### [48] [Memento-Skills: Let Agents Design Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18743)
*Huichi Zhou,Siyuan Guo,Anjie Liu,Zhongwei Yu,Ziqin Gong,Bowen Zhao,Zhixun Chen,Menglong Zhang,Yihang Chen,Jinsong Li,Runyu Yang,Qiangbin Liu,Xinlei Yu,Jianmin Zhou,Na Wang,Chunyang Sun,Jun Wang*

TL;DR: 提出了Memento-Skills，一个基于记忆强化学习框架的通用、可持续学习的LLM智能体系统，通过外部化技能的演化实现无需更新LLM参数的持续学习，在两个基准测试上分别取得了26.2%和116.2%的相对准确率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖人工设计的智能体，缺乏自主构建、适应和改进任务特定智能体的能力。研究旨在开发一个能够作为"智能体设计智能体"的通用系统，通过经验实现端到端的智能体设计与持续改进。

Method: 基于Memento 2的读-写反思学习机制：在读阶段，行为可训练的技能路由器根据当前状态提示选择最相关技能；在写阶段，智能体基于新经验更新和扩展技能库。系统使用结构化markdown文件存储可复用技能作为持久化、可演化的记忆。

Result: 在General AI Assistants基准测试上取得了26.2%的相对准确率提升，在Humanity's Last Exam上取得了116.2%的相对准确率提升。实验结果表明该系统能够通过迭代式的技能生成和优化持续提升自身能力。

Abstract: We introduce \emph{Memento-Skills}, a generalist, continually-learnable LLM agent system that functions as an \emph{agent-designing agent}: it autonomously constructs, adapts, and improves task-specific agents through experience. The system is built on a memory-based reinforcement learning framework with \emph{stateful prompts}, where reusable skills (stored as structured markdown files) serve as persistent, evolving memory. These skills encode both behaviour and context, enabling the agent to carry forward knowledge across interactions.
  Starting from simple elementary skills (like Web search and terminal operations), the agent continually improves via the \emph{Read--Write Reflective Learning} mechanism introduced in \emph{Memento~2}~\cite{wang2025memento2}. In the \emph{read} phase, a behaviour-trainable skill router selects the most relevant skill conditioned on the current stateful prompt; in the \emph{write} phase, the agent updates and expands its skill library based on new experience. This closed-loop design enables \emph{continual learning without updating LLM parameters}, as all adaptation is realised through the evolution of externalised skills and prompts.
  Unlike prior approaches that rely on human-designed agents, Memento-Skills enables a generalist agent to \emph{design agents end-to-end} for new tasks. Through iterative skill generation and refinement, the system progressively improves its own capabilities. Experiments on the \emph{General AI Assistants} benchmark and \emph{Humanity's Last Exam} demonstrate sustained gains, achieving 26.2\% and 116.2\% relative improvements in overall accuracy, respectively. Code is available at https://github.com/Memento-Teams/Memento-Skills.

</details>


### [49] [NeuroGame Transformer: Gibbs-Inspired Attention Driven by Game Theory and Statistical Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18761)
*Djamel Bouchaffra,Fayçal Ykhlef,Hanene Azzag,Mustapha Lebbah,Bilal Faye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出NeuroGame Transformer (NGT)，通过将注意力机制重构为博弈论与统计物理的统一框架（合作博弈+Ising模型），利用Shapley值和Banzhaf指数量化Token重要性，有效解决了标准Transformer难以建模高阶Token依赖的问题，在NLI任务上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer的注意力机制基于成对（pairwise）公式，这种形式限制了其对Token之间高阶依赖关系的建模能力。为了突破这一局限，作者希望重新定义注意力机制，使其能够捕捉更复杂的交互关系。

Method: 本文提出了NeuroGame Transformer (NGT)：1. 双重视角：将Token同时视为合作博弈中的玩家和统计物理系统中的自旋；2. 重要性量化：使用Shapley值（全局置换归因）和Banzhaf指数（局部联盟影响），通过可学习的门控参数结合形成外部磁场；3. 能量建模：利用Ising哈密顿量定义系统能量，注意力权重通过平均场方程在Gibbs分布下作为边缘概率高效计算；4. 可扩展性：提出重要性加权蒙特卡洛估计器，避免显式指数因子，确保长序列的数值稳定性，并提供理论收敛保证。

Result: 实验结果表明，NGT在SNLI和MNLI-matched数据集上表现强劲，超越了一些主要的高效Transformer基线模型。在SNLI上，测试准确率达到86.4%（峰值验证准确率86.6%），超越了ALBERT-Base，并与RoBERTa-Base保持了高度竞争力。

Conclusion: NeuroGame Transformer成功地将博弈论与统计物理概念融入注意力机制，为建模高阶Token依赖提供了新范式。该方法不仅在理论上具有收敛保证和公平性-敏感性权衡的特性，还在实际NLI任务中展示了卓越性能，为Transformer架构的改进提供了新思路。

Abstract: Standard attention mechanisms in transformers are limited by their pairwise formulation, which hinders the modeling of higher-order dependencies among tokens. We introduce the NeuroGame Transformer (NGT) to overcome this by reconceptualizing attention through a dual perspective: tokens are treated simultaneously as players in a cooperative game and as interacting spins in a statistical physics system. Token importance is quantified using two complementary game-theoretic concepts -- Shapley values for global, permutation-based attribution and Banzhaf indices for local, coalition-level influence. These are combined via a learnable gating parameter to form an external magnetic field, while pairwise interaction potentials capture synergistic relationships. The system's energy follows an Ising Hamiltonian, with attention weights emerging as marginal probabilities under the Gibbs distribution, efficiently computed via mean-field equations. To ensure scalability despite the exponential coalition space, we develop importance-weighted Monte Carlo estimators with Gibbs-distributed weights. This approach avoids explicit exponential factors, ensuring numerical stability for long sequences. We provide theoretical convergence guarantees and characterize the fairness-sensitivity trade-off governed by the interpolation parameter. Experimental results demonstrate that the NeuroGame Transformer achieves strong performance across SNLI, and MNLI-matched, outperforming some major efficient transformer baselines. On SNLI, it attains a test accuracy of 86.4\% (with a peak validation accuracy of 86.6\%), surpassing ALBERT-Base and remaining highly competitive with RoBERTa-Base. Code is available at https://github.com/dbouchaffra/NeuroGame-Transformer.

</details>


### [50] [A Concept is More Than a Word: Diversified Unlearning in Text-to-Image Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18767)
*Duc Hao Pham,Van Duy Truong,Duy Khanh Dinh,Tien Cuong Nguyen,Dien Hy Ngo,Tuan Anh Bui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Diversified Unlearning方法，通过使用多样化的提示集合替代单一关键词来表示概念，从而在文本到图像扩散模型中实现更精确、鲁棒的概念遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于关键词的概念遗忘方法存在固有局限性：视觉概念是多维的，可以用多种文本形式表达，且在潜在空间中常与相关概念重叠。单一关键词只能代表概念的狭窄点估计，无法覆盖其完整的语义分布，导致遗忘过程脆弱且容易过度遗忘。

Method: 提出了Diversified Unlearning框架，该框架不依赖单一关键词，而是通过一组上下文多样化的提示来表示一个概念，从而获得更丰富的语义表示，实现更精确和鲁棒的遗忘。

Result: 实验表明，该方法作为现有遗忘流程的附加组件，能够实现更强的概念擦除效果、更好地保留无关概念，并对对抗性恢复攻击具有更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 基于分布的多样化提示表示方法优于传统的单一关键词方法，为扩散模型的概念遗忘提供了一个更有效、更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Concept unlearning has emerged as a promising direction for reducing the risks of harmful content generation in text-to-image diffusion models by selectively erasing undesirable concepts from a model's parameters. Existing approaches typically rely on keywords to identify the target concept to be unlearned. However, we show that this keyword-based formulation is inherently limited: a visual concept is multi-dimensional, can be expressed in diverse textual forms, and often overlap with related concepts in the latent space, making keyword-only unlearning, which imprecisely indicate the target concept is brittle and prone to over-forgetting. This occurs because a single keyword represents only a narrow point estimate of the concept, failing to cover its full semantic distribution and entangled variations in the latent space. To address this limitation, we propose Diversified Unlearning, a distributional framework that represents a concept through a set of contextually diverse prompts rather than a single keyword. This richer representation enables more precise and robust unlearning. Through extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks and state-of-the-art baselines, we demonstrate that integrating Diversified Unlearning as an add-on component into existing unlearning pipelines consistently achieves stronger erasure, better retention of unrelated concepts, and improved robustness against adversarial recovery attacks.

### [52] [dTRPO: Trajectory Reduction in Policy Optimization of Diffusion Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18806)
*Wenxuan Zhang,Lemeng Wu,Changsheng Zhao,Ernie Chang,Mingchen Zhuge,Zechun Liu,Andy Su,Hanxian Huang,Jun Chen,Chong Zhou,Raghuraman Krishnamoorthi,Vikas Chandra,Mohamed Elhoseiny,Wei Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Trajectory Reduction Policy Optimization (dTRPO)方法，通过减少轨迹概率计算成本来改进扩散大语言模型的策略优化，在多项任务上取得了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散大语言模型(dLLMs)引入了新的语言生成范式，但在与人类偏好对齐方面面临新的挑战，特别是在策略优化过程中轨迹概率计算成本高昂，限制了离线策略训练的规模化。

Method: 提出两种轨迹缩减策略：(1)在参考策略正则化下，证明新解掩码tokens的概率比是中间扩散状态的无偏估计；(2)通过重新掩码最终状态的单次前向传播有效估计完整轨迹概率。将这些策略整合到策略优化目标中，提出dTRPO方法。

Result: 在7B规模的dLLMs上进行评估，dTRPO显著提升了模型性能：STEM任务提升高达9.6%，编程任务提升高达4.3%，指令遵循任务提升高达3.0%。同时展现出高效的训练效率和生成效率。

Conclusion: dTRPO方法成功解决了dLLMs策略优化中的轨迹概率计算成本问题，实现了高效的离线单次前向训练，在保持训练效率的同时显著提升了模型在多个任务上的性能表现。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) introduce a new paradigm for language generation, which in turn presents new challenges for aligning them with human preferences. In this work, we aim to improve the policy optimization for dLLMs by reducing the cost of the trajectory probability calculation, thereby enabling scaled-up offline policy training. We prove that: (i) under reference policy regularization, the probability ratio of the newly unmasked tokens is an unbiased estimate of that of intermediate diffusion states, and (ii) the probability of the full trajectory can be effectively estimated with a single forward pass of a re-masked final state. By integrating these two trajectory reduction strategies into a policy optimization objective, we propose Trajectory Reduction Policy Optimization (dTRPO). We evaluate dTRPO on 7B dLLMs across instruction-following and reasoning benchmarks. Results show that it substantially improves the core performance of state-of-the-art dLLMs, achieving gains of up to 9.6% on STEM tasks, up to 4.3% on coding tasks, and up to 3.0% on instruction-following tasks. Moreover, dTRPO exhibits strong training efficiency due to its offline, single-forward nature, and achieves improved generation efficiency through high-quality outputs.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于强化学习的大型语言模型智能体推理方法受到终端奖励稀疏的限制，难以进行细粒度的状态级优化；而过程奖励模型虽然可行，但训练专用奖励模型计算成本高且扩展困难。

Method: 提出RewardFlow方法，通过构建推理轨迹中状态的状态图，分析各状态对任务成功的贡献，并采用拓扑感知的图传播机制量化这些贡献，从而生成客观的状态级奖励信号。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) holds significant promise for enhancing the agentic reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) with external environments. However, the inherent sparsity of terminal rewards hinders fine-grained, state-level optimization. Although process reward modeling offers a promising alternative, training dedicated reward models often entails substantial computational costs and scaling difficulties. To address these challenges, we introduce RewardFlow, a lightweight method for estimating state-level rewards tailored to agentic reasoning tasks. RewardFlow leverages the intrinsic topological structure of states within reasoning trajectories by constructing state graphs. This enables an analysis of state-wise contributions to success, followed by topology-aware graph propagation to quantify contributions and yield objective, state-level rewards. When integrated as dense rewards for RL optimization, RewardFlow substantially outperforms prior RL baselines across four agentic reasoning benchmarks, demonstrating superior performance, robustness, and training efficiency. The implementation of RewardFlow is publicly available at https://github.com/tmlr-group/RewardFlow.

### [56] [Conflict-Based Search for Multi Agent Path Finding with Asynchronous Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18866)
*Xuemian Wu,Shizhe Zhao,Zhongqiang Ren*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CBS-AA算法，解决了现有连续时间冲突搜索（CCBS）不完备的理论缺陷，在异步动作多智能体路径规划（MAPF-AA）问题中实现了完备性和最优性保证，并通过冲突消解技术显著提升了算法的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出异步动作冲突搜索算法（CBS-AA），通过理论手段规避连续等待时间带来的不可数无限状态空间问题，保证算法的完备性和解的最优性。在此基础上，开发多种冲突消解技术以进一步提升算法的可扩展性。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提方法能够将搜索分支数量减少高达90%，验证了CBS-AA算法及其冲突消解技术在异步动作场景下的有效性和效率提升。

Abstract: Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) seeks collision-free paths for multiple agents from their respective start locations to their respective goal locations while minimizing path costs. Most existing MAPF algorithms rely on a common assumption of synchronized actions, where the actions of all agents start at the same time and always take a time unit, which may limit the use of MAPF planners in practice. To get rid of this assumption, Continuous-time Conflict-Based Search (CCBS) is a popular approach that can find optimal solutions for MAPF with asynchronous actions (MAPF-AA). However, CCBS has recently been identified to be incomplete due to an uncountably infinite state space created by continuous wait durations. This paper proposes a new method, Conflict-Based Search with Asynchronous Actions (CBS-AA), which bypasses this theoretical issue and can solve MAPF-AA with completeness and solution optimality guarantees. Based on CBS-AA, we also develop conflict resolution techniques to improve the scalability of CBS-AA further. Our test results show that our method can reduce the number of branches by up to 90%.

### [58] [Reasoning over mathematical objects: on-policy reward modeling and test time aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18886)

Abstract: The ability to precisely derive mathematical objects is a core requirement for downstream STEM applications, including mathematics, physics, and chemistry, where reasoning must culminate in formally structured expressions. Yet, current LM evaluations of mathematical and scientific reasoning rely heavily on simplified answer formats such as numerical values or multiple choice options due to the convenience of automated assessment. ### [59] [Quantitative Introspection in Language Models: Tracking Internal States Across Conversation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18893)
*Nicolas Martorell*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 受心理学启发，本研究提出利用大语言模型（LLM）的数值自我报告来追踪其对话过程中的内部情感状态。研究发现，通过基于logit的自我报告方法，可以有效追踪探针定义的内部状态（Spearman ρ = 0.40-0.76），该方法随模型规模扩展效果提升，最高可达 R² ≈ 0.93，为对话AI系统的内部状态监测提供了一种可行的补充工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 追踪大语言模型在对话过程中的内部状态对安全性、可解释性和模型福利至关重要。然而现有方法（如线性探针等白盒方法）在压缩高维表示时不完美，且随着模型规模增大更难应用。研究从人类心理学中数值自我报告这一广泛使用的工具获得灵感，探索LLM自身的数值自我报告是否能追踪探针定义的情感状态随时间的变化。

Method: 受人类心理学中数值自我报告方法的启发，研究者将其应用于LLM内部状态追踪。研究选取四个概念对（wellbeing、interest、focus和impulsivity），在40个十轮对话中进行实验。将内省操作化为模型自我报告与概念匹配的探针定义内部状态之间的因果信息耦合。采用基于logit的自我报告方法替代贪婪解码，并使用激活操控验证因果性。

Result: 实验结果表明：1）贪婪解码的自我报告会坍缩为少数无信息量的值，但基于logit的自我报告能有效揭示内省能力；2）该指标能有效追踪可解释的内部状态，在LLaMA-3.2-3B-Instruct上达到Spearman ρ = 0.40-0.76，等渗R² = 0.12-0.54；3）激活操控证实了这种耦合具有因果性；4）内省能力在对话第一轮即存在但随对话演变；5）选择性操控可提升内省能力（ΔR²最高达0.30）；6）该方法随模型规模扩展，在LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct上接近R² ≈ 0.93，并在其他模型家族中部分复现。

Conclusion: 数值自我报告是一种可行且互补的工具，用于追踪对话AI系统中的内部情感状态，为AI安全性、可解释性和模型福利研究提供了新的方法论支持。

Abstract: Tracking the internal states of large language models across conversations is important for safety, interpretability, and model welfare, yet current methods are limited. Linear probes and other white-box methods compress high-dimensional representations imperfectly and are harder to apply with increasing model size. Taking inspiration from human psychology, where numeric self-report is a widely used tool for tracking internal states, we ask whether LLMs' own numeric self-reports can track probe-defined emotive states over time. We study four concept pairs (wellbeing, interest, focus, and impulsivity) in 40 ten-turn conversations, operationalizing introspection as the causal informational coupling between a model's self-report and a concept-matched probe-defined internal state. We find that greedy-decoded self-reports collapse outputs to few uninformative values, but introspective capacity can be unmasked by calculating logit-based self-reports. This metric tracks interpretable internal states (Spearman $ρ= 0.40$-$0.76$; isotonic $R^2 = 0.12$-$0.54$ in LLaMA-3.2-3B-Instruct), follows how those states change over time, and activation steering confirms the coupling is causal. Furthermore, we find that introspection is present at turn 1 but evolves through conversation, and can be selectively improved by steering along one concept to boost introspection for another ($ΔR^2$ up to $0.30$). Crucially, these phenomena scale with model size in some cases, approaching $R^2 \approx 0.93$ in LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct, and partially replicate in other model families. Together, these results position numeric self-report as a viable, complementary tool for tracking internal emotive states in conversational AI systems.

### [60] [Secure Linear Alignment of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18908)
*Matt Gorbett,Suman Jana*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种隐私保护的跨模型推理框架，利用不同语言模型之间的表征收敛特性，通过仿射变换和同态加密技术，在不共享数据或模型的情况下实现了跨孤岛推理，在保证安全性的同时实现了亚秒级延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型之间日益显现出表征收敛现象——即使训练目标、架构和数据模态不同，模型仍学习到相似的表征。这种独立训练模型之间的兼容性为跨模型对齐提供了新机会，特别是在安全、隐私或竞争约束下禁止直接数据或模型共享的场景中。

Method: 提出了一种隐私保护框架，在共享公共数据集上学习仿射变换，并在推理过程中应用同态加密来保护客户端查询。通过仅加密线性对齐和分类操作，在保证安全性的同时实现了低延迟推理。研究还系统探究了独立模型最终隐藏状态之间的线性变换。

Result: 实验表明：跨模型线性映射在嵌入分类和分布外检测任务上表现良好，性能损失极小；首次证明了线性对齐有时能够在独立训练的模型之间实现文本生成。所提框架通过仅加密线性对齐和分类操作，实现了亚秒级推理延迟，同时保持了强安全保证。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了利用表征收敛现象进行隐私保护跨模型推理的可行性，为在安全、隐私或竞争约束下无法直接共享数据或模型的场景开辟了新的应用领域，同时也展示了跨模型对齐在生成任务上的潜力。

Abstract: Language models increasingly appear to learn similar representations, despite differences in training objectives, architectures, and data modalities. This emerging compatibility between independently trained models introduces new opportunities for cross-model alignment to downstream objectives. Moreover, it unlocks new potential application domains, such as settings where security, privacy, or competitive constraints prohibit direct data or model sharing. In this work, we propose a privacy-preserving framework that exploits representational convergence to enable cross-silo inference between independent language models. The framework learns an affine transformation over a shared public dataset and applies homomorphic encryption to protect client queries during inference. By encrypting only the linear alignment and classification operations, the method achieves sub-second inference latency while maintaining strong security guarantees. We support this framework with an empirical investigation into representational convergence, in which we learn linear transformations between the final hidden states of independent models. We evaluate these cross-model mappings on embedding classification and out-of-distribution detection, observing minimal performance degradation across model pairs. Additionally, we show for the first time that linear alignment sometimes enables text generation across independently trained models.

Abstract: This paper presents a manifesto that articulates the conceptual foundations of Agentic Business Process Management (APM), an extension of Business Process Management (BPM) for governing autonomous agents executing processes in organizations. From a management perspective, APM represents a paradigm shift from the traditional process view of the business process, driven by the realization of process awareness and an agent-oriented abstraction, where software and human agents act as primary functional entities that perceive, reason, and act within explicit process frames. This perspective marks a shift from traditional, automation-oriented BPM toward systems in which autonomy is constrained, aligned, and made operational through process awareness.
  We introduce the core abstractions and architectural elements required to realize APM systems and elaborate on four key capabilities that such APM agents must support: framed autonomy, explainability, conversational actionability, and self-modification. These capabilities jointly ensure that agents' goals are aligned with organizational goals and that agents behave in a framed yet proactive manner in pursuing those goals. We discuss the extent to which the capabilities can be realized and identify research challenges whose resolution requires further advances in BPM, AI, and multi-agent systems. The manifesto thus serves as a roadmap for bridging these communities and for guiding the development of APM systems in practice.

Abstract: Structural causal models (SCMs) were conceived to formulate and answer causal questions. We review limitations of previous approaches to modeling such agents, and then introduce intentional interventions, a new time-agnostic operator that induces a twin SCM we call a structural final model (SFM). SFMs treat observed values as the outcome of intentional interventions and relate them to the counterfactual conditions of those interventions (what would have happened had the agent not intervened). We show how SFMs can be used to empirically detect agents and to discover their intentions.

### [63] [Evaluating 5W3H Structured Prompting for Intent Alignment in Human-AI Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18976)
*Peng Gang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出基于5W3H的结构化意图表示框架PPS，通过多模型多任务对比实验发现，自然语言渲染的PPS在意图对齐指标上优于简单提示词和原始JSON格式，尤其在高模糊性任务中效果显著，能减少66.1%的后续追问轮次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言提示词经常遭受意图传输损失问题，即用户实际需求与向AI系统传达内容之间存在差距，需要一种结构化的意图表示方法来改善人机交互中的意图对齐。

Method: 采用控制性三条件实验设计，在三个领域（商业、技术、旅行）的60个任务中，使用三个大型语言模型（DeepSeek-V3、Qwen-Max、Kimi），对比三种提示条件：（A）简单提示词、（B）原始PPS JSON、（C）自然语言渲染的PPS；收集540个AI生成输出，使用LLM评判器进行评估；引入以用户意图为中心的评估维度goal_alignment。

Result: 实验结果表明：自然语言渲染的PPS在goal_alignment指标上优于简单提示词和原始JSON；PPS的效果具有任务依赖性，在高模糊性的商业分析任务中提升显著，但在低模糊性的旅行规划任务中效果相反；揭示了标准LLM评估中的测量不对称性问题；初步回顾性调查显示后续追问轮次从3.33减少至1.13（降低66.1%）。

Conclusion: 结构化意图表示可以改善人机交互中的对齐和可用性，特别是在用户意图本身具有模糊性的任务中；PPS框架为解决意图传输损失问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Natural language prompts often suffer from intent transmission loss: the gap between what users actually need and what they communicate to AI systems. We evaluate PPS (Prompt Protocol Specification), a 5W3H-based framework for structured intent representation in human-AI interaction. In a controlled three-condition study across 60 tasks in three domains (business, technical, and travel), three large language models (DeepSeek-V3, Qwen-Max, and Kimi), and three prompt conditions - (A) simple prompts, (B) raw PPS JSON, and (C) natural-language-rendered PPS - we collect 540 AI-generated outputs evaluated by an LLM judge. We introduce goal_alignment, a user-intent-centered evaluation dimension, and find that rendered PPS outperforms both simple prompts and raw JSON on this metric. PPS gains are task-dependent: gains are large in high-ambiguity business analysis tasks but reverse in low-ambiguity travel planning. We also identify a measurement asymmetry in standard LLM evaluation, where unconstrained prompts can inflate constraint adherence scores and mask the practical value of structured prompting. A preliminary retrospective survey (N = 20) further suggests a 66.1% reduction in follow-up prompts required, from 3.33 to 1.13 rounds. These findings suggest that structured intent representations can improve alignment and usability in human-AI interaction, especially in tasks where user intent is inherently ambiguous.

### [64] [Unmasking Algorithmic Bias in Predictive Policing: A GAN-Based Simulation Framework with Multi-City Temporal Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18987)
*Pronob Kumar Barman,Pronoy Kumar Barman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验揭示了极端且年度变化的偏见：巴尔的摩检测模式下2019年平均DIR高达15714，芝加哥对黑人居民存在中度检测不足（DIR=0.22），所有条件下基尼系数持续在0.43-0.62。CTGAN去偏见方法只能部分重新分配检测率，无法消除结构性差异。社会经济回归分析证实社区种族构成与检测可能性强相关（白人百分比r=0.83，黑人百分比r=-0.81）。敏感性分析显示结果对警员部署水平最为敏感。

Conclusion: 预测性警务系统存在显著的种族偏见传播问题，单纯的技术去偏见干预不足以消除结构性差异，必须配合政策干预才能解决根本问题。警员部署水平是影响偏见结果的最敏感因素。

Abstract: Predictive policing systems that direct patrol resources based on algorithmically generated crime forecasts have been widely deployed across US cities, yet their tendency to encode and amplify racial disparities remains poorly understood in quantitative terms. We present a reproducible simulation framework that couples a Generative Adversarial Network GAN with a Noisy OR patrol detection model to measure how racial bias propagates through the full enforcement pipeline from crime occurrence to police contact. Using 145000 plus Part 1 crime records from Baltimore 2017 to 2019 and 233000 plus records from Chicago 2022, augmented with US Census ACS demographic data, we compute four monthly bias metrics across 264 city year mode observations: the Disparate Impact Ratio DIR, Demographic Parity Gap, Gini Coefficient, and a composite Bias Amplification Score.
  Our experiments reveal extreme and year variant bias in Baltimores detected mode, with mean annual DIR up to 15714 in 2019, moderate under detection of Black residents in Chicago DIR equals 0.22, and persistent Gini coefficients of 0.43 to 0.62 across all conditions. We further demonstrate that a Conditional Tabular GAN CTGAN debiasing approach partially redistributes detection rates but cannot eliminate structural disparity without accompanying policy intervention. Socioeconomic regression analysis confirms strong correlations between neighborhood racial composition and detection likelihood Pearson r equals 0.83 for percent White and r equals negative 0.81 for percent Black. A sensitivity analysis over patrol radius, officer count, and citizen reporting probability reveals that outcomes are most sensitive to officer deployment levels. The code and data are publicly available at this repository.

### [65] [Evaluating Game Difficulty in Tetris Block Puzzle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18994)
*Chun-Jui Wang,Jian-Ting Guo,Hung Guei,Chung-Chin Shih,Ti-Rong Wu,I-Chen Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文利用随机Gumbel AlphaZero（SGAZ）算法评估Tetris Block Puzzle不同规则集的难度，发现增加保留和预览数量会降低难度，而增加方块变体（特别是T-pentomino）会增加难度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tetris Block Puzzle及其流行变体拥有数千万下载量，但缺乏对规则集难度的原则性评估。受此前利用AlphaZero评估国际象棋变体研究的启发，本文旨在填补这一空白，系统研究该领域的难度评估问题。

Method: 采用随机Gumbel AlphaZero（SGAZ）算法作为预算感知规划智能体，以训练奖励和收敛迭代次数等为评估指标，系统性地比较不同规则变体（包括保留方块h、预览保留方块p以及额外的俄罗斯方块变体）对游戏难度的影响。

Abstract: Tetris Block Puzzle is a single player stochastic puzzle in which a player places blocks on an 8 x 8 grid to complete lines; its popular variants have amassed tens of millions of downloads. Despite this reach, there is little principled assessment of which rule sets are more difficult. Inspired by prior work that uses AlphaZero as a strong evaluator for chess variants, we study difficulty in this domain using Stochastic Gumbel AlphaZero (SGAZ), a budget-aware planning agent for stochastic environments. We evaluate rule changes including holding block h, preview holding block p, and additional Tetris block variants using metrics such as training reward and convergence iterations. Empirically, increasing h and p reduces difficulty (higher reward and faster convergence), while adding more Tetris block variants increases difficulty, with the T-pentomino producing the largest slowdown. Through analysis, SGAZ delivers strong play under small simulation budgets, enabling efficient, reproducible comparisons across rule sets and providing a reference for future design in stochastic puzzle games.

</details>


### [66] [Regret Bounds for Competitive Resource Allocation with Endogenous Costs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18999)
*Rui Chai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了在线资源分配中内生成本的影响，证明了竞争性分配策略在对抗性环境中可实现O(√T log N)的最优遗憾界，并揭示了交互拓扑结构对计算-遗憾权衡的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在线优化假设成本是外生的，但实际模块化系统中资源分配成本依赖于完整分配向量（通过编码模块间合作与竞争关系的交互矩阵W），这种内生成本特性带来了根本性挑战。作者旨在理解这种内生性如何影响不同分配范式的性能，并为去中心化竞争性分配提供理论依据。

Method: 分析了三种分配范式：(I)均匀分配（成本无关），(II)门控分配（成本估计），(III)基于乘性权重更新的竞争性分配（成本揭示）。建立了对抗性序列下有界变化的严格遗憾分离分析框架，并研究了交互矩阵W的拓扑结构（全连接、稀疏拓扑、环形拓扑如五行拓扑）对计算复杂度与遗憾权衡的影响。

Result: 在对抗性序列下证明了严格的性能分离：均匀分配遗憾为Ω(T)，门控分配为O(T^{2/3})，竞争性分配为O(√T log N)。揭示了拓扑结构的关键作用：全交互(|E|=O(N²))遗憾最紧但每步成本高，稀疏拓扑(|E|=O(N))遗憾仅增加O(√log N)但计算成本从O(N²)降至O(N)，同时包含合作与竞争链接的环形拓扑（如五行拓扑）最小化计算×遗憾乘积。

Conclusion: 首次为模块化架构中去中心化竞争性分配提供了严格的遗憾理论依据，确立了成本内生性是区别于部分可观测性的基本挑战。交互拓扑的拓扑结构提供了计算-遗憾权衡的设计空间，为实际系统设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We study online resource allocation among N interacting modules over T rounds. Unlike standard online optimization, costs are endogenous: they depend on the full allocation vector through an interaction matrix W encoding pairwise cooperation and competition.
  We analyze three paradigms: (I) uniform allocation (cost-ignorant), (II) gated allocation (cost-estimating), and (III) competitive allocation via multiplicative weights update with interaction feedback (cost-revealing). Our main results establish a strict separation under adversarial sequences with bounded variation: uniform incurs Omega(T) regret, gated achieves O(T^{2/3}), and competitive achieves O(sqrt(T log N)). The performance gap stems from competitive allocation's ability to exploit endogenous cost information revealed through interactions.
  We further show that W's topology governs a computation-regret tradeoff. Full interaction (|E|=O(N^2)) yields the tightest bound but highest per-step cost, while sparse topologies (|E|=O(N)) increase regret by at most O(sqrt(log N)) while reducing per-step cost from O(N^2) to O(N). Ring-structured topologies with both cooperative and competitive links - of which the five-element Wuxing topology is canonical - minimize the computation x regret product.
  These results provide the first formal regret-theoretic justification for decentralized competitive allocation in modular architectures and establish cost endogeneity as a fundamental challenge distinct from partial observability.
  Keywords: online learning, regret bounds, resource allocation, endogenous costs, interaction topology, multiplicative weights, modular systems, Wuxing topology

</details>

*Jonah Leshin,Manish Shah,Ian Timmis,Daniel Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了Stability Monitor，一种黑盒监控系统，用于检测AI模型端点的行为一致性变化，发现传统可靠性指标无法捕捉的模型身份漂移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI应用的稳定性依赖于模型端点的行为一致性，但传统的可靠性指标（如正常运行时间、延迟和吞吐量）无法捕捉模型行为的改变。模型端点可能因权重更新、分词器、量化、推理引擎等变化而在保持“健康”状态的同时，其实际模型身份已发生改变。

Method: 提出Stability Monitor黑盒监控系统，通过周期性地从固定提示集中采样输出并随时间比较输出分布来对端点进行指纹识别。使用跨提示的求和能量距离统计量比较指纹，通过排列检验p值作为分布偏移的证据，并按顺序聚合以检测变化事件并定义稳定期。

Result: 在受控验证中，Stability Monitor成功检测到了模型家族、版本、推理栈、量化和行为参数的变化。在对多个提供商托管的同一模型进行真实世界监控时，观察到了显著的提供商之间和提供商内部的稳定性差异。

Conclusion: Stability Monitor能够有效检测AI模型端点的行为变化，填补了传统可靠性指标无法捕捉模型身份漂移的空白，为AI应用的稳定性监控提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: The consistency of AI-native applications depends on the behavioral consistency of the model endpoints that power them. Traditional reliability metrics such as uptime, latency and throughput do not capture behavioral change, and an endpoint can remain "healthy" while its effective model identity changes due to updates to weights, tokenizers, quantization, inference engines, kernels, caching, routing, or hardware. We introduce Stability Monitor, a black-box stability monitoring system that periodically fingerprints an endpoint by sampling outputs from a fixed prompt set and comparing the resulting output distributions over time. Fingerprints are compared using a summed energy distance statistic across prompts, with permutation-test p-values as evidence of distribution shift aggregated sequentially to detect change events and define stability periods. In controlled validation, Stability Monitor detects changes to model family, version, inference stack, quantization, and behavioral parameters. In real-world monitoring of the same model hosted by multiple providers, we observe substantial provider-to-provider and within-provider stability differences.

Using criminal justice risk assessment as a focal case, we conduct a synthetic review connecting three intertwined aspects of AI's role in judicial decision-making: the performance and fairness of AI tools, the strengths and biases of human judges, and the nature of AI+human interactions. Across the fields of computer science, economics, law, criminology and psychology, researchers have made significant progress in evaluating the predictive validity of automated risk assessment instruments, documenting biases in judicial decision-making, and, to a more limited extent, examining how judges use algorithmic recommendations. While the existing empirical evidence indicates that the impact of AI decision aid tools on pretrial and sentencing decisions is modest or inexistent, our review also reveals important gaps in the canvassed literatures. Further research is needed to evaluate the performance of AI risk assessment instruments, understand how judges navigate noisy decision making environments and how individual characteristics influence judges' responses to AI advice. We argue that AI vs Human comparisons have the potential to yield new insights into both algorithmic tools and human decision-makers and advocate greater interdisciplinary integration and cross-fertilization in future research.

### [69] [Serendipity by Design: Evaluating the Impact of Cross-domain Mappings on Human and LLM Creativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19087)
*Qiawen Ella Liu,Marina Dubova,Henry Conklin,Takumi Harada,Thomas L. Griffiths*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型（LLM）是否具有与人类相似的创造力机制，以及相同的创造力干预手段（跨域映射）能否同样提升两者的创意表现，从而理解远程联想在创造性思维中的作用及人机差异。

Method: 让人类参与者和LLM为十种日常产品生成新颖特征，对比两种提示条件：(i)跨域映射，要求从随机分配的远程源域（如章鱼、仙人掌、GPS）迁移属性至目标产品；(ii)用户需求，要求针对未满足的用户需求提出创新。通过系统操纵源域与目标域的语义距离，评估干预效果。

Result: 人类可靠地从随机分配的跨域映射中获益，创造力显著提升；LLM平均创意水平高于人类，但跨域映射未产生统计学显著效果。然而，当灵感源与目标产品的语义距离增大时，跨域映射对人类和LLM的影响均增强。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了远程联想在创造性构思中的重要作用，同时指出人类与LLM在响应相同创造力干预时存在系统性差异：人类更依赖外部类比启发，而LLM本身具备较高原创性且对跨域映射干预敏感度较低。

Abstract: Are large language models (LLMs) creative in the same way humans are, and can the same interventions increase creativity in both? We evaluate a promising but largely untested intervention for creativity: forcing creators to draw an analogy from a random, remote source domain (''cross-domain mapping''). Human participants and LLMs generated novel features for ten daily products (e.g., backpack, TV) under two prompts: (i) cross-domain mapping, which required translating a property from a randomly assigned source (e.g., octopus, cactus, GPS), and (ii) user-need, which required proposing innovations targeting unmet user needs. We show that humans reliably benefit from randomly assigned cross-domain mappings, while LLMs, on average, generate more original ideas than humans and do not show a statistically significant effect of cross-domain mappings. However, in both systems, the impact of cross-domain mapping increases when the inspiration source becomes more semantically distant from the target. Our results highlight both the role of remote association in creative ideation and systematic differences in how humans and LLMs respond to the same intervention for creativity.

### [70] [LuMamba: Latent Unified Mamba for Electrode Topology-Invariant and Efficient EEG Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19100)
*Danaé Broustail,Anna Tegon,Thorir Mar Ingolfsson,Yawei Li,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了LuMamba，一种结合拓扑不变编码和线性复杂度状态空间建模的自监督EEG基础模型框架，在多个下游任务上达到SOTA性能，同时计算效率提升377倍，支持12倍长序列处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出LuMamba框架：1）使用LUNA的learned-query cross-attention机制实现通道统一，解决电极拓扑差异问题；2）采用FEMBA的双向Mamba块实现高效时间建模，具有线性复杂度；3）首次系统研究Latent-Euclidean Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (LeJEPA)用于生物信号学习；4）结合masked reconstruction和LeJEPA两种预训练目标；5）在TUEG语料库的21,000+小时无标注EEG数据上进行自监督预训练。

Result: 模型仅含4.6M参数，在TUAB上达到80.99%平衡准确率，在阿尔茨海默病检测上达到0.97 AUPR的SOTA性能。相比现有SOTA模型：1）在相同序列长度下需要377×更少的FLOPS；2）可处理12×更长的序列。预训练目标研究发现：单独使用masked reconstruction产生结构化但泛化性较低的表示，单独使用LeJEPA产生弥散的嵌入，两者结合效果最佳。

Conclusion: LuMamba成功解决了EEG基础模型中的电极拓扑差异和计算可扩展性问题，通过创新的架构设计和预训练策略，在保持轻量化（4.6M参数）的同时实现了卓越的性能和效率，为EEG基础模型的发展提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) enables non-invasive monitoring of brain activity across clinical and neurotechnology applications, yet building foundation models for EEG remains challenging due to \emph{differing electrode topologies} and \emph{computational scalability}, as Transformer architectures incur quadratic sequence complexity. As a joint solution, we propose \textbf{LuMamba} (\textbf{L}atent \textbf{U}nified \textbf{Mamba}), a self-supervised framework combining topology-invariant encodings with linear-complexity state-space modeling, using LUNA's learned-query cross-attention mechanism for channel unification~\cite{luna}, and FEMBA's bidirectional Mamba blocks for efficient temporal modeling~\cite{femba}. Within this architecture, we provide the first systematic investigation of the Latent-Euclidean Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (LeJEPA) for biosignal learning. Pre-trained on over 21,000 hours of unlabeled EEG from the TUEG corpus, LuMamba is evaluated on five downstream tasks spanning abnormality detection, artifact recognition, and mental condition classification across electrode configurations ranging from 16 to 26 channels. In the pre-training objective, masked reconstruction alone yields structured but less generalizable representations, while LeJEPA alone produces diffuse embeddings; combining both objectives achieves the most robust performance. With only 4.6M parameters, LuMamba attains 80.99\% balanced accuracy on TUAB and achieves state-of-art performance on Alzheimer's detection (0.97 AUPR), while requiring \textbf{377$\times$ fewer FLOPS} than state-of-art models at equivalent sequence lengths and scaling to \textbf{12$\times$ longer sequences} before reaching typical GPU memory limits. Code is available at https://github.com/pulp-bio/biofoundation

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 自一致性和言语化置信度均随样本数扩展，但自一致性初始判别能力较低，中等采样规模下落后于言语化置信度。混合估计器仅需两个样本即可平均提升AUROC达+12，即使扩展到更大预算也优于单一信号。数学领域作为RLVR风格后训练的原生域，推理模型的不确定性质量更高、互补性更强且扩展更快。

Abstract: Uncertainty estimation is critical for deploying reasoning language models, yet remains poorly understood under extended chain-of-thought reasoning. We study parallel sampling as a fully black-box approach using verbalized confidence and self-consistency. Across three reasoning models and 17 tasks spanning mathematics, STEM, and humanities, we characterize how these signals scale.
  Both self-consistency and verbalized confidence scale in reasoning models, but self-consistency exhibits lower initial discrimination and lags behind verbalized confidence under moderate sampling. Most uncertainty gains, however, arise from signal combination: with just two samples, a hybrid estimator improves AUROC by up to $+12$ on average and already outperforms either signal alone even when scaled to much larger budgets, after which returns diminish. These effects are domain-dependent: in mathematics, the native domain of RLVR-style post-training, reasoning models achieve higher uncertainty quality and exhibit both stronger complementarity and faster scaling than in STEM or humanities.

### [72] [Implicit Patterns in LLM-Based Binary Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19138)
*Qiang Li,XiangRui Zhang,Haining Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文首次在大规模追踪层面研究了多轮LLM二进制漏洞分析，发现LLM推理过程会自发形成四种结构化的token级隐式模式（早期剪枝、路径依赖锁定、目标回溯、知识引导优先），这些模式构成了LLM推理的隐式抽象机制，而非显式的控制流或预定义启发式规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大规模追踪级别的分析方法，对521个二进制文件进行分析，收集了99,563个推理步骤的数据。通过分析推理轨迹，识别和分类token级别的隐式模式，研究这些模式如何组织和调节探索过程。

Result: 通过对521个二进制文件和99,563个推理步骤的大规模追踪分析，研究发现多轮LLM推理会产生四种主要的token级隐式模式：早期剪枝、路径依赖锁定、目标回溯、知识引导优先。这些模式通过隐式决策调节路径选择、承诺和修正，形成了一个稳定的、结构化的系统，具有独特的时序角色和可测量的特征。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了对LLM驱动的二进制分析的首次系统性描述，证明了LLM推理过程能够自发形成稳定、结构化的隐式模式系统，这为构建更可靠的分析系统奠定了基础。这些发现对于理解和改进LLM在复杂分析任务中的行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: Binary vulnerability analysis is increasingly performed by LLM-based agents in an iterative, multi-pass manner, with the model as the core decision-maker. However, how such systems organize exploration over hundreds of reasoning steps remains poorly understood, due to limited context windows and implicit token-level behaviors. We present the first large-scale, trace-level study showing that multi-pass LLM reasoning gives rise to structured, token-level implicit patterns. Analyzing 521 binaries with 99,563 reasoning steps, we identify four dominant patterns: early pruning, path-dependent lock-in, targeted backtracking, and knowledge-guided prioritization that emerge implicitly from reasoning traces. These token-level implicit patterns serve as an abstraction of LLM reasoning: instead of explicit control-flow or predefined heuristics, exploration is organized through implicit decisions regulating path selection, commitment, and revision. Our analysis shows these patterns form a stable, structured system with distinct temporal roles and measurable characteristics. Our results provide the first systematic characterization of LLM-driven binary analysis and a foundation for more reliable analysis systems.

### [73] [D5P4: Partition Determinantal Point Process for Diversity in Parallel Discrete Diffusion Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19146)

Motivation: 离散扩散模型是文本生成中自回归方法的有力替代方案，但其解码方法研究不足。现有的自回归解码方法（如束搜索）无法直接应用于迭代去噪过程，而现有的扩散解码技术对批内多样性的控制能力有限。

Method: 提出了一个针对离散扩散的广义束搜索框架，支持并行生成候选和模块化束选择目标。作为专注于多样性的实例，提出了D5P4方法，将选择步骤建模为行列式点过程（DPP）上的最大后验概率（MAP）推理，利用可扩展的贪婪求解器，实现了多GPU兼容性与模型概率和目标多样性之间的显式权衡。

Result: 在自由形式生成和问答任务上的实验表明，D5P4在保持具有竞争力的生成质量的同时，相比强基线显著提高了生成多样性，且计算开销几乎为零。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了离散扩散模型解码方法的空白，证明了在扩散模型中引入可控且高效的多样性解码机制是可行的，为非自回归文本生成提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are promising alternatives to autoregressive approaches for text generation, yet their decoding methods remain under-studied. Standard decoding methods for autoregressive models, such as beam search, do not directly apply to iterative denoising, and existing diffusion decoding techniques provide limited control over in-batch diversity. To bridge this gap, we introduce a generalized beam-search framework for discrete diffusion that generates candidates in parallel and supports modular beam-selection objectives. As a diversity-focused instantiation, we propose D5P4, which formulates the selection step as MAP inference over a Determinantal Point Process. Leveraging a scalable greedy solver, D5P4 maintains multi-GPU compatibility and enables an explicit trade-off between model probability and target diversity with near-zero compute overhead. Experiments on free-form generation and question answering demonstrate that D5P4 improves diversity over strong baselines while maintaining competitive generation quality.

</details>


### [74] [Box Maze: A Process-Control Architecture for Reliable LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19182)
*Zou Qiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Box Maze框架，通过引入显式的认知控制架构（记忆锚定、结构化推理、边界执行三层），将大模型在对抗性攻击下的边界失效成功率从约40%降低至1%以下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在对抗性提示下易产生幻觉和不可靠推理；现有安全方法（如RLHF和输出过滤）主要在行为层面操作，缺乏强制推理过程完整性的显式架构机制。

Method: 提出Box Maze概念过程控制架构，将LLM推理分解为记忆锚定、结构化推理和边界执行三个显式层；基于仿真的评估方法，在DeepSeek-V3、Doubao、Qwen等异构LLM系统上，采用渐进式边界侵蚀场景进行对抗性测试。

Result: 在n=50的对抗性场景仿真实验中，该架构约束将边界失效成功率从基线RLHF的约40%降低至1%以下；显式认知控制层提高了多异构LLM系统在边界维护上的一致性。

Conclusion: 过程级控制是提升大语言模型推理可靠性的有前途方向；仿真结果初步证明了显式架构机制在对抗条件下的有效性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong generative capabilities but remain vulnerable to hallucination and unreliable reasoning under adversarial prompting. Existing safety approaches -- such as reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and output filtering -- primarily operate at the behavioral level and may lack explicit architectural mechanisms for enforcing reasoning process integrity.
  This paper proposes the Box Maze framework, a conceptual process-control architecture that decomposes LLM reasoning into three explicit layers: memory grounding, structured inference, and boundary enforcement. We introduce preliminary simulation-based evaluation involving progressive boundary erosion scenarios across multiple heterogeneous LLM systems (DeepSeek-V3, Doubao, Qwen). Results from n=50 adversarial scenarios suggest that explicit cognitive control layers may improve consistency in boundary maintenance, with architectural constraints reducing boundary failure rates from approximately 40% (baseline RLHF) to below 1% under adversarial conditions.
  While current validation is simulation-based, these preliminary results indicate that process-level control may offer a promising direction for improving reliability in large language model reasoning.

### [75] [OS-Themis: A Scalable Critic Framework for Generalist GUI Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19191)
*Zehao Li,Zhenyu Wu,Yibo Zhao,Bowen Yang,Jingjing Xie,Zhaoyang Liu,Zhoumianze Liu,Kaiming Jin,Jianze Liang,Zonglin Li,Feng Wu,Bowen Zhou,Zun Wang,Zichen Ding*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习有潜力提升GUI智能体在随机环境中的鲁棒性，但训练对奖励函数质量高度敏感，现有奖励方法难以同时实现可扩展性和性能。

Method: 提出OS-Themis多智能体评论框架：将轨迹分解为可验证的里程碑以隔离关键决策证据，并引入审查机制严格审核证据链后再做出最终裁决；同时构建了跨平台GUI结果奖励基准OmniGUIRewardBench (OGRBench) 用于评估。

Result: 在AndroidWorld实验中，OS-Themis用于在线RL训练时带来10.3%的性能提升，用于自训练循环的轨迹验证与过滤时带来6.9%的提升；在OGRBench基准上，所有评估模型在OS-Themis框架下均达到最佳性能。

Conclusion: OS-Themis证明了多智能体评论框架在GUI智能体奖励设计中的有效性，能够同时实现可扩展性与准确性，为智能体进化提供了有力的技术支撑。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has the potential to improve the robustness of GUI agents in stochastic environments, yet training is highly sensitive to the quality of the reward function. Existing reward approaches struggle to achieve both scalability and performance. To address this, we propose OS-Themis, a scalable and accurate multi-agent critic framework. Unlike a single judge, OS-Themis decomposes trajectories into verifiable milestones to isolate critical evidence for decision making and employs a review mechanism to strictly audit the evidence chain before making the final verdict. To facilitate evaluation, we further introduce OmniGUIRewardBench (OGRBench), a holistic cross-platform benchmark for GUI outcome rewards, where all evaluated models achieve their best performance under OS-Themis. Extensive experiments on AndroidWorld show that OS-Themis yields a 10.3% improvement when used to support online RL training, and a 6.9% gain when used for trajectory validation and filtering in the self-training loop, highlighting its potential to drive agent evolution.

### [76] [A Vision-based Framework for Intelligent gNodeB Mobility Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18092)

Result: 基于真实视觉数据和仿真无线环境的实验结果表明，该方法相比静态基站将视距阻塞持续时间减少了高达75%，验证了在无线接入网中集成多模态感知与基于学习的控制方案的可行性。

Conclusion: 研究证实了将视觉感知与学习控制集成到RAN架构中的有效性，为动态环境下的智能移动基站控制提供了可行的技术路径。

These SMs extend state-of-the-art O-RAN-based architectures by enabling the transmission of vision-based sensing data and gNB positioning control messages. The second is an O-RAN xApp, VisionApp, which fuses vision and radio data, and uses this information to control the position of a mobile gNB, using a Deep Q-Network (DQN). The third is a digital twin environment, VisionTwin, which incorporates vision data and can emulate realistic wireless scenarios; this digital twin was used to train the DQN running in VisionApp and validate the overall system. Experimental results, obtained using real vision data and an emulated radio, demonstrate that the proposed approach reduces the duration of Line-of-Sight (LoS) blockages by up to 75% compared to a static gNB. These findings confirm the viability of integrating multimodal perception and learning-based control within RANs.

The results demonstrate the potential of using RISs in mobile networks to enhance radio signal quality in urban environments through strategic placements. Our findings suggest that RISs can significantly mitigate Path Loss (PL) and improve signal coverage in challenging urban environments, particularly in areas where traditional base station deployment alone would be insufficient. Furthermore, the study highlights the role of RISs in reducing the need for additional base stations, thereby optimizing network costs and infrastructure while maintaining high-quality service delivery. The insights gained from this research provide valuable guidelines for network planners and engineers seeking to implement RIS technology in future 5G and beyond networks, ensuring more efficient and robust urban communication systems.

Method: 提出RUBICONe框架，将RAFT共识算法扩展至无线通信环境，实现多车分布式共识；利用多个软件定义无线电（SDR）设备搭建实验平台，使多车能够协同处理并聚合各自的感知数据。

By implementing a distributed consensus framework that extends the RAFT algorithm with wireless connectivity, RUBICONe enables multiple vehicles to collectively process and aggregate their perceptions. Using multiple software-defined radio (SDR) devices as the experimental platform, this study demonstrates how consensus-based decision-making significantly reduces the impact of environmental interference and mitigates the risk of misjudgments by individual vehicles. Just as crossing the Rubicone marked a point of irrevocable action backed by collective intelligence, RUBICONe ensures that lane change decisions are made with comprehensive situational awareness and distributed consensus, showcasing the reliability gain of consensus in wireless communications.

### [80] [Cross-Layer Traffic Allocation and Contention Window Optimization for Wi-Fi 7 MLO: When DRL Meets LSTM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18602)
*Zhang Liu,Xianbin Wang,Shumin Lian,Lianfen Huang,Liqun Fu,Ying-Jun Angela Zhang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种跨层优化框架，通过联合优化Wi-Fi 7多链路操作（MLO）中的流量分配和初始竞争窗口大小，并设计LSTM-SAC算法求解，显著提升了网络吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wi-Fi 7标准引入了多链路操作（MLO）以支持跨多个频段的并发通信，其双层MAC架构（U-MAC与L-MAC）的内在耦合以及无线网络的动态复杂性使得MLO优化极具挑战性，需要一种能够协同优化两层决策的有效方法。

Method: 扩展单链路Bianchi Markov模型构建分析框架以刻画网络吞吐量、流量分配与初始竞争窗口（ICW）尺寸的关系；在此基础上建立非凸非线性跨层优化问题；设计基于长短期记忆网络的软演员-评论家（LSTM-SAC）算法，利用LSTM处理Wi-Fi网络中的部分可观测性与非马尔可夫动态特性以高效求解。

Result: 基于事件驱动Wi-Fi仿真器的实验表明，所提LSTM-SAC算法在广泛网络设置下显著优于现有基准方案，有效提升了网络吞吐量。

Conclusion: 所提出的跨层优化框架与LSTM-SAC算法成功解决了Wi-Fi 7 MLO中U-MAC与L-MAC的耦合优化难题，为未来多样化应用提供了高效的多链路通信支持。

Abstract: To support future diverse applications, multi-link operation (MLO) has been introduced in the Wi-Fi 7 standard (IEEE 802.11be) to enable concurrent communication over multiple frequency bands. This new capability relies on a two-tier medium access control (MAC) architecture, where the upper MAC (U-MAC) allocates traffic across links and the lower MAC (L-MAC) performs independent channel access. However, MLO optimization is challenging due to the inherent coupling between the U-MAC and L-MAC, as well as the dynamic and complex nature of wireless networks. To address these challenges, we propose a cross-layer framework that jointly optimizes traffic allocation at the U-MAC layer and initial contention window (ICW) sizes at the L-MAC layer to maximize network throughput. Specifically, we extend the single-link Bianchi Markov model to develop an analytical framework that captures the relationship among network throughput, traffic allocation, and ICW sizes. Based on this framework, we formulate a nonconvex, nonlinear cross-layer optimization problem. To solve it efficiently, we design a long short-term memory-based soft actor-critic (LSTM-SAC) algorithm that leverages LSTM to handle the partial observability and non-Markovian dynamics inherent in Wi-Fi networks. Finally, using a well-developed event-based Wi-Fi simulator, we demonstrate that the proposed LSTM-SAC substantially outperforms existing benchmark solutions across a wide range of network settings.

</details>

Method: AutORAN构建了一个全自动的xApp生成流水线，集成了多个功能模块，包括用户需求引导、AI/ML功能设计与验证，以及xApp的合成与部署。该框架无需人工编码或测试，即可将高层用户意图转化为可快速部署的xApp。

Result: 在代表性xApp任务上的综合评估表明，AutORAN生成的xApp能够达到甚至超越已知最佳手工基准的性能，同时显著加速了从需求获取到部署的整个开发周期。

To lower the barrier of xApp development for both developers and network operators, we present AutORAN, the first LLM-driven natural language programming framework for agile xApps that automates the entire xApp development pipeline. In a nutshell, AutORAN turns high-level user intents into swiftly deployable xApps within minutes, eliminating the need for manual coding or testing. To this end, AutORAN builds a fully automated xApp generation pipeline, which integrates multiple functional modules (from user requirement elicitation, AI/ML function design and validation, to xApp synthesis and deployment). We design, implement, and comprehensively evaluate AutORAN on representative xApp tasks. Results show AutORAN-generated xApps can achieve similar or even better performance than the best known hand-crafted baselines. AutORAN drastically accelerates the xApp development cycle (from user intent elicitation to roll-out), streamlining O-RAN innovation.

### [82] [Masking Intent, Sustaining Equilibrium: Risk-Aware Potential Game-empowered Two-Stage Mobile Crowdsensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18670)
*Houyi Qi,Minghui Liwang,Kaiwen Tan,Wenyong Wang,Sai Zou,Yiguang Hong,Xianbin Wang,Wei Ni*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出iParts框架，通过两阶段服务供给机制解决动态移动群智感知中的意图隐私泄露和任务执行风险问题，在保护工人意图隐私的同时实现了高效可靠的感知任务分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有移动群智感知系统面临三个关键挑战：1）诚实但好奇的平台可能通过重复观察和频率分析推断工人的意图/偏好隐私；2）工人退出和执行不确定性导致覆盖不稳定和冗余感知；3）重复的全局在线重优化产生高昂交互开销并扩大可观察攻击面。

Method: 提出两阶段服务供给框架iParts：离线阶段采用带记忆化/永久随机化的个性化本地差分隐私技术对工人意图向量进行扰动，平台基于扰动意图构建冗余感知质量模型，并在预算、个体理性、质量失败风险和意图失配风险约束下进行风险感知预规划，将其建模为精确势博弈；在线阶段通过临时招募势博弈对空闲/待命工人进行轻量级补救，实现有限交互轮次和低可观察性。

Result: 实验表明iParts实现了良好的隐私-效用-效率权衡，相比代表性基线方法，在提高社会福利和任务完成率的同时，降低了冗余度和通信开销。

Conclusion: iParts框架成功解决了动态移动群智感知中意图隐私保护和任务执行可靠性之间的矛盾，通过离线预规划与在线补救的协同机制，在保护隐私的前提下实现了高效稳定的感知服务供给，为复杂应用场景下的移动群智感知系统设计提供了新的解决思路。

Abstract: Beyond data collection, future mobile crowdsensing (MCS) in complex applications must satisfy diverse requirements, including reliable task completion, budget and quality constraints, and fluctuating worker availability. Besides raw-data and location privacy, workers' intent/preference traces can be exploited by an honest-but-curious platform, enabling intent inference from repeated observations and frequency profiling. Meanwhile, worker dropouts and execution uncertainty may cause coverage instability and redundant sensing, while repeated global online re-optimization incurs high interaction overhead and enlarges the observable attack surface. To address these issues, we propose iParts, an intent-preserving and risk-controllable two-stage service provisioning framework for dynamic MCS. In the offline stage, workers report perturbed intent vectors via personalized local differential privacy with memorization/permanent randomization, suppressing frequency-based inference while preserving decision utility. Using only perturbed intents, the platform builds a redundancy-aware quality model and performs risk-aware pre-planning under budget, individual rationality, quality-failure risk, and intent-mismatch risk constraints. We formulate offline pre-planning as an exact potential game with expected social welfare as the potential function, ensuring a constrained pure-strategy Nash equilibrium and finite-step convergence under asynchronous feasible improvements. In the online stage, when runtime dynamics cause quality deficits, a temporary-recruitment potential game over idle/standby workers enables lightweight remediation with bounded interaction rounds and low observability. Experiments show that iParts achieves a favorable privacy-utility-efficiency trade-off, improving welfare and task completion while reducing redundancy and communication overhead compared with representative baselines.

### [83] [Holistic Energy Performance Management: Enablers, Capabilities, and Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18841)
*Meysam Masoudi,Milad Ganjalizadeh,Tahar Zanouda,Pal Frenger*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文指出5G网络中的节能特性孤立激活时效果欠佳，提出了一种特性编排器来协调信令调度与休眠模式等特性，在几乎不损失吞吐量的情况下显著降低了基站能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能耗是移动网络运营商的重大关切，也是6G标准发展的重要目标。然而，现有5G新空口（NR）网络中的众多节能特性在独立激活时仅能带来次优的节能效果，且往往会牺牲覆盖范围或延迟等其他关键性能指标（KPI），因此亟需一种协调机制来优化整体能效。

Method: 首先提出了一种紧凑的分类法，将硬件能力与高层特性区分开来，并将其分为两类：创造空闲窗口的信令与调度机制，以及利用这些窗口节能的特性。随后，引入了一个特性编排器作为逻辑节点，用于协调这些特性以最大化节能收益。研究使用符合3GPP标准的仿真器和产品级真实参数进行了验证。

Result: 仿真结果表明，与未协调的场景相比，协调使用精益NR、调度机制和先进休眠模式能显著降低gNodeB（gNB）的能耗，且吞吐量的损失微乎其微。

Conclusion: 研究证明了跨特性协调对于最大化网络节能至关重要。最后，论文概述了能效性能管理在可观测性、系统动力学、协调机制及智能自动化方面的开放性问题与未来研究方向。

Abstract: Energy consumption is a significant concern for mobile network operators, and to enable further network energy improvements it is also an important target when developing the emerging 6G standard. In this paper we show that, despite the existence of many energy-saving features in 5G new radio (NR) networks, activating them in isolation yields only suboptimal savings and often compromises other network key performance indicators (KPIs) such as coverage or latency. We first introduce a compact taxonomy that distinguishes hardware capabilities from higher-layer features. Features fall into two classes: (i) signaling and scheduling mechanisms that create idle windows, and (ii) features that utilize those windows to save energy. We then present a feature orchestrator as a logical node to coordinate between features to maximize the gain. Using a 3GPP-aligned simulator with product-realistic parameters, we show that coordinating lean NR, scheduling, and advanced sleep modes significantly reduces gNodeB (gNB) energy consumption with negligible throughput loss, compared to the uncoordinated scenario. We conclude by outlining open issues in observability, system dynamics, coordination, and intelligent automation for energy performance management.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲神经网络(SNNs)具有高能效和事件驱动计算特性，适合低功耗边缘AI应用，但其FPGA硬件实现面临计算量大、内存占用高和灵活性有限等挑战。

Method: 提出集成RISC-V控制器和事件驱动SNN核心的SoC架构：采用二值化权重将乘法器替换为位运算；引入脉冲时间排序器处理活跃脉冲；通过跳过非信息性事件减少计算。

This paper proposes a compact System-on-Chip (SoC) architecture for temporal-coding SNNs, integrating a RISC-V controller with an event-driven SNN core. It replaces multipliers with bitwise operations using binarized weights, includes a spike-time sorter for active spikes, and skips noninformative events to reduce computation. The architecture runs fully on a Xilinx Artix-7 FPGA, achieving up to 16x memory reduction for weights and lowering computational overhead and latency, with 97.0% accuracy on MNIST and 88.3% on FashionMNIST. This self-contained design provides an efficient, scalable platform for real-time neuromorphic inference at the edge.

### [85] [HWE-Bench: Can Language Models Perform Board-level Schematic Designs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18102)
*Weibo Qiu,Yinhao Xiao,Runyu Pan*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为\hweb的评估框架，用于基准测试大语言模型在板级电路设计任务中的表现。该框架包含300个设计任务和2914个真实IC数据手册，评估结果显示，表现最好的模型总体通过率仅为8.15%，表明当前模型虽具备工程可用性，但缺乏物理直觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在软件开发、数字逻辑生成等工程任务中表现出了巨大潜力，但其在板级电路设计方面的能力尚未得到充分研究。板级电路设计需要对现实世界物理和集成电路（IC）数据手册有协同理解，而IC数据手册包含各组件的详细规格。

Method: 提出了一个名为\hweb的评估框架，该框架包含从GitHub和OSHWLab等开源和众包平台提取的300个板级设计任务，涵盖8个应用领域，并配有2914个真实IC数据手册的知识库。对于每个任务，LLM需要根据提供的电路功能需求和组件数据手册，从头开始生成原理图。生成的原理图将经过静态电气规则检查，然后传递给电路模拟器以验证其动态行为。

Result: 评估结果显示，尽管当前模型在初始工程可用性和文档理解方面表现良好，但它们缺乏物理直觉。表现最好的模型总体通过率仅为8.15%。

Conclusion: 本文认为，\hweb的进步将为实用的电子设计自动化（EDA）智能体的开发铺平道路，从而彻底改变板级设计领域。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated significant potential in various engineering tasks, including software development, digital logic generation, and companion document maintenance. However, their ability to perform board-level circuit design is understudied, as this task requires a synergized understanding of real-world physics and Integrated Circuit (IC) datasheets, the latter comprising detailed specifications for individual components. To address this challenge, we propose \hweb, an evaluation framework that benchmarks the ability of LLMs to perform such designs. It consists of 300 board-level design tasks pulled from open-source and crowdsourcing platforms such as GitHub and OSHWLab, covering 8 application domains, and is complemented with a knowledge base of 2,914 real IC datasheets. For each task, the LLMs are tasked with generating a schematic from scratch, using the provided circuit functional requirements and a set of component datasheets as input. The resulting schematic will be checked against a static electrical rules, and then passed to a circuit simulator to verify its dynamic behavior. Our evaluation show that although current models achieve initial engineering usability and documentation understanding, they lack physical intuition, as the top-performing model achieved an overall pass rate of 8.15\%. We envision that advancements on \hweb\ will pave the way for the development of practical Electronic Design Automation (EDA) agents, revolutionizing the field of board-level design.

### [86] [A Survey of Neural Network Variational Monte Carlo from a Computing Workload Characterization Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18126)
*Zhengze Xiao,Xuanzhe Ding,Yuyang Lou,Lixue Cheng,Chaojian Li*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文对四种代表性神经网络变分蒙特卡洛(NNVMC)方法进行了首次系统性的GPU负载分析与性能表征，揭示了低强度逐元素运算和数据移动内核是主要瓶颈，并提出了算法-硬件协同设计的优化方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NNVMC作为解决量子多体问题的有效方法虽能实现具有竞争力的精度，但在GPU上的实际部署受限于高昂的运行时和内存开销。与语言和视觉负载不同，NNVMC包含MCMC采样、波函数构建和导数/拉普拉斯算子评估等物理特定阶段，产生异构的内核行为和非平凡瓶颈，缺乏对其负载特性的深入理解。

Method: 采用统一分析协议，对PauliNet、FermiNet、Psiformer和Orbformer四种代表性波函数拟设进行研究。从模型层面分析运行时和内存趋势，在内核层面通过家族分解、算术强度、Roofline定位和硬件利用率计数器分析内核行为。

Result: 端到端性能通常受限于低强度的逐元素运算和数据移动内核，计算/内存平衡在不同波函数拟设和阶段间存在显著差异。内核行为呈现高度异构性，不同拟设的负载特征各异。

Conclusion: 基于发现提出了可扩展NNVMC系统的算法-硬件协同设计启示，包括相位感知调度、以内存为中心的优化和异构加速策略，为未来NNVMC系统的性能优化提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Neural Network Variational Monte Carlo (NNVMC) has emerged as a promising paradigm for solving quantum many-body problems by combining variational Monte Carlo with expressive neural-network wave-function ansätze. Although NNVMC can achieve competitive accuracy with favorable asymptotic scaling, practical deployment remains limited by high runtime and memory cost on modern graphics processing units (GPUs). Compared with language and vision workloads, NNVMC execution is shaped by physics-specific stages, including Markov-Chain Monte Carlo sampling, wave-function construction, and derivative/Laplacian evaluation, which produce heterogeneous kernel behavior and nontrivial bottlenecks. This paper provides a workload-oriented survey and empirical GPU characterization of four representative ansätze: PauliNet, FermiNet, Psiformer, and Orbformer. Using a unified profiling protocol, we analyze model-level runtime and memory trends and kernel-level behavior through family breakdown, arithmetic intensity, roofline positioning, and hardware utilization counters. The results show that end-to-end performance is often constrained by low-intensity elementwise and data-movement kernels, while the compute/memory balance varies substantially across ansätze and stages. Based on these findings, we discuss algorithm--hardware co-design implications for scalable NNVMC systems, including phase-aware scheduling, memory-centric optimization, and heterogeneous acceleration.

</details>


### [87] [WarPGNN: A Parametric Thermal Warpage Analysis Framework with Physics-aware Graph Neural Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18581)
*Haotian Lu,Jincong Lu,Sachin Sachdeva,Sheldon X. -D. Tan*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了WarPGNN框架，利用图神经网络实现高效的参数化热翘曲分析，相比传统FEM方法加速超过20万倍，且在精度上保持可比性（归一化RMSE仅1.26%），同时具备良好的跨配置迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着系统级封装和基于芯粒的设计以及异构2.5D/3D集成技术的发展，热致翘曲已成为关键的可靠性问题。传统数值方法虽能提供高精度结果，但计算成本极高，限制了其在复杂芯粒-封装系统中的可扩展性。

Method: 该方法首先将多芯片版图编码为简化传递闭包图(rTCG)，然后使用基于图卷积网络(GCN)的编码器提取层次结构特征，最后通过U-Net启发的解码器从图特征嵌入重构翘曲图。为解决翘曲数据分布的长尾问题，开发了物理信息损失函数，并基于图同构网络(GIN)改进了消息传递编码器。

Result: 实验结果表明，WarPGNN相比2D高效FEM方法加速205.91倍，相比3D FEM方法COMSOL加速119766.64倍，同时保持仅1.26%的归一化RMSE和2.21%的翘曲值误差；相比DeepONet模型，训练时间降低3.4倍；在未见过的数据集上归一化RMSE仅为3.69%。

Conclusion: WarPGNN成功解决了传统数值方法计算成本高的问题，实现了快速且准确的热翘曲分析，为复杂chiplet-package系统的翘曲感知版图探索提供了可行方案。该方法在保持高精度的同时显著降低了计算开销，并展现出良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: With the advent of system-in-package (SiP) chiplet-based design and heterogeneous 2.5D/3D integration, thermal-induced warpage has become a critical reliability concern. While conventional numerical approaches can deliver highly accurate results, they often incur prohib- itively high computational costs, limiting their scalability for complex chiplet-package systems. In this paper, we present WarPGNN, an ef- ficient and accurate parametric thermal warpage analysis framework powered by Graph Neural Networks (GNNs). By operating directly on graphs constructed from the floorplans, WarPGNN enables fast warpage-aware floorplan exploration and exhibits strong transfer- ability across diverse package configurations. Our method first en- codes multi-die floorplans into reduced Transitive Closure Graphs (rTCGs), then a Graph Convolution Network (GCN)-based encoder extracts hierarchical structural features, followed by a U-Net inspired decoder that reconstructs warpage maps from graph feature embed- dings. Furthermore, to address the long-tailed pattern of warpage data distribution, we developed a physics-informed loss and revised a message-passing encoder based on Graph Isomorphic Network (GIN) that further enhance learning performance for extreme cases and expressiveness of graph embeddings. Numerical results show that WarPGNN achieves more than 205.91x speedup compared with the 2-D efficient FEM-based method and over 119766.64x acceleration with 3-D FEM method COMSOL, respectively, while maintaining comparable accuracy at only 1.26% full-scale normalized RMSE and 2.21% warpage value error. Compared with recent DeepONet-based model, our method achieved comparable prediction accuracy and in- ference speedup with 3.4x lower training time. In addition, WarPGNN demonstrates remarkable transferability on unseen datasets with up to 3.69% normalized RMSE and similar runtime.

</details>


### [88] [Mitigating the Bandwidth Wall via Data-Streaming System-Accelerator Co-Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19057)
*Qunyou Liu,Marina Zapater,David Atienza*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 提出了一种面向Transformer推理的系统-加速器协同设计方法，通过分页流式数据流和计算传输重叠优化，在真实系统约束下实现了最高22倍加速，证明了分页流水和重叠机制比大容量片上SRAM更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型虽然革新了AI领域，但其巨大的计算和内存需求给硬件加速带来挑战。实际中端到端吞吐量往往受限于分页数据移动和互连带宽，而非原始MAC计数，这促使研究者从系统集成的角度重新审视加速器设计。

Method: 硬件层面设计了MatrixFlow加速器，采用松耦合的16×16脉动阵列架构，使用4KB分页对齐的块矩阵乘法、约20KB小片上缓冲区以及DMA-计算-DMA输出的流水线调度；系统层面开发了Gem5-AcceSys全系统模拟器扩展，支持PCIe等标准互连和多种内存层次配置（直接内存、直接缓存、设备内存模式），并考虑SMMU/TLB效应。

Result: 在BERT和ViT等代表性Transformer模型上的gem5仿真实验表明：相比纯CPU基线实现最高22倍端到端加速，相比最先进的松耦合和紧耦合加速器获得5-8倍性能提升；基于PCIe的标准主机内存设计可达到片上HBM约80%的性能。

Conclusion: 在真实系统约束下，分页流式传输和流水线重叠机制比大容量本地SRAM更能有效提升Transformer推理效率，为硬件加速器设计提供了新的设计思路。

Abstract: Transformers have revolutionized AI in natural language processing and computer vision, but their large computation and memory demands pose major challenges for hardware acceleration. In practice, end-to-end throughput is often limited by paged data movement and interconnect bandwidth rather than raw MAC count. This work proposes a unified system-accelerator co-design approach for transformer inference that jointly optimizes a matrix accelerator and its system integration through paged streaming dataflows and explicit overlap of compute and transfer. On the hardware side, we introduce MatrixFlow, a loosely coupled 16x16 systolic-array accelerator with a page-aligned block matrix multiplication method using 4 KB tiles, a small on-chip buffer of about 20 KB, and a pipelined schedule of DMA, compute, and DMA-out to utilize interconnect bandwidth efficiently. On the system side, we develop Gem5-AcceSys, an extension of the gem5 full-system simulator that explores standard interconnects such as PCIe and configurable memory hierarchies including Direct Memory, Direct Cache, and Device Memory modes with SMMU/TLB effects. We evaluate the co-design using gem5 simulations on representative transformer models including BERT and ViT across multiple data types and system setups. Results show up to 22x end-to-end speedup over a CPU-only baseline and 5x to 8x gains over state-of-the-art loosely and tightly coupled accelerators. We further show that a standard PCIe-based host-memory design can achieve about 80 percent of the performance of on-device HBM. Overall, paged streaming and pipeline overlap, rather than large local SRAMs, are the most effective levers for efficient transformer inference under realistic system constraints.

</details>

# cs.OS [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [Quine: Realizing LLM Agents as Native POSIX Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18030)
*Hao Ke*

Main category: cs.OS

TL;DR: Quine将LLM代理实现为原生POSIX进程，利用操作系统的成熟机制（隔离、调度、通信）替代应用层编排，实现了进程级隔离、组合与资源控制，并揭示了POSIX模型在认知任务中的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理框架在应用层重新实现隔离、调度和通信机制，而这些功能操作系统内核已经成熟提供。这种重复实现增加了复杂性且错失了系统级优势。

Method: 设计运行时架构Quine，将LLM代理显式映射到POSIX进程原语：身份→PID、接口→标准流和退出状态、状态→内存/环境变量/文件系统、生命周期→fork/exec/exit。通过单个可执行文件递归派生新实例实现该模型。参考实现已开源。

Result: Quine成功将LLM代理映射到POSIX进程模型（PID为身份、标准流为接口、内存/文件系统为状态、fork/exec/exit为生命周期），通过递归派生自身实例实现。系统继承了内核的隔离、组合和资源控制能力，支持递归委托、exec上下文更新和shell原生组合。同时识别出POSIX模型的不足：进程提供稳健的执行基础，但缺少完整的认知运行时模型，需要扩展任务相对世界和可修正时间机制。

Conclusion: Quine证明了将LLM代理建立在操作系统进程模型的可行性，避免了应用层重复造轮子。更重要的是，它清晰地揭示了进程模型在认知任务中的边界——虽然提供了可靠的执行载体，但缺少任务相对世界和可修正时间等认知特性。这为未来研究指明了方向。

Abstract: Current LLM agent frameworks often implement isolation, scheduling, and communication at the application layer, even though these mechanisms are already provided by mature operating systems. Instead of introducing another application-layer orchestrator, this paper presents Quine, a runtime architecture and reference implementation that realizes LLM agents as native POSIX processes. The mapping is explicit: identity is PID, interface is standard streams and exit status, state is memory, environment variables, and filesystem, and lifecycle is fork/exec/exit. A single executable implements this model by recursively spawning fresh instances of itself. By grounding the agent abstraction in the OS process model, Quine inherits isolation, composition, and resource control directly from the kernel, while naturally supporting recursive delegation, context renewal via exec, and shell-native composition. The design also exposes where the POSIX process model stops: processes provide a robust substrate for execution, but not a complete runtime model for cognition. In particular, the analysis points toward two immediate extensions beyond process semantics: task-relative worlds and revisable time. A reference implementation of Quine is publicly available on GitHub.

</details>
